\DoxyCodeLine{02647\ TEST(AllOfTest,\ ExplainsResult)\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{02649\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02650\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Successful\ match.\ \ Both\ matchers\ need\ to\ explain.\ \ The\ second}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02651\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ matcher\ doesn't\ give\ an\ explanation,\ so\ only\ the\ first\ matcher's}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02656\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Successful\ match.\ \ Both\ matchers\ need\ to\ explain.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02659\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Explain(m,\ 30));}
\DoxyCodeLine{02660\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02661\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Successful\ match.\ \ All\ matchers\ need\ to\ explain.\ \ The\ second}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02662\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ matcher\ doesn't\ given\ an\ explanation.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02665\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Explain(m,\ 25));}
\DoxyCodeLine{02666\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02667\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Successful\ match.\ \ All\ matchers\ need\ to\ explain.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02668\ \ \ m\ =\ AllOf(GreaterThan(10),\ GreaterThan(20),\ GreaterThan(30));}
\DoxyCodeLine{02669\ \ \ EXPECT\_EQ(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}which\ is\ 30\ more\ than\ 10,\ and\ which\ is\ 20\ more\ than\ 20,\ "{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02670\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}and\ which\ is\ 10\ more\ than\ 30"{}},}

\DoxyCodeLine{02672\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02673\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Failed\ match.\ \ The\ first\ matcher,\ which\ failed,\ needs\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02674\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ explain.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02675\ \ \ m\ =\ AllOf(GreaterThan(10),\ GreaterThan(20));}
\DoxyCodeLine{02676\ \ \ EXPECT\_EQ(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}which\ is\ 5\ less\ than\ 10"{}},\ Explain(m,\ 5));}
\DoxyCodeLine{02677\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02678\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Failed\ match.\ \ The\ second\ matcher,\ which\ failed,\ needs\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02679\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ explain.\ \ Since\ it\ doesn't\ given\ an\ explanation,\ nothing\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02680\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ printed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02681\ \ \ m\ =\ AllOf(GreaterThan(10),\ Lt(30));}
